Initialization function for the Q15 FIR filter. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em S} & points to an instance of the Q15 FIR filter structure. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em num\+Taps} & Number of filter coefficients in the filter. Must be even and greater than or equal to 4. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em p\+Coeffs} & points to the filter coefficients. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em p\+State} & points to the state buffer. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em block\+Size} & number of samples that are processed at a time. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The function returns either {\ttfamily ARM\+\_\+\+MATH\+\_\+\+SUCCESS} if initialization was successful or {\ttfamily ARM\+\_\+\+MATH\+\_\+\+ARGUMENT\+\_\+\+ERROR} if {\ttfamily num\+Taps} is not a supported value.
\end{DoxyReturn}
For the MVE version, the coefficient length must be a multiple of 8. You can pad with zeros if you have less coefficients. \Hypertarget{filtering__functions_8h_a23ef4b2597aecc4d43cce7c4b456ae71}\index{filtering\_functions.h@{filtering\_functions.h}!arm\_fir\_init\_q31@{arm\_fir\_init\_q31}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{arm__math__types_8h_a5e459c6409dfcd2927bb8a57491d7cf6}{arm\+\_\+status}} arm\+\_\+fir\+\_\+interpolate\+\_\+init\+\_\+f32 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structarm__fir__interpolate__instance__f32}{arm\+\_\+fir\+\_\+interpolate\+\_\+instance\+\_\+f32}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{S}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{L}{, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{num\+Taps}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{arm__math__types_8h_a4611b605e45ab401f02cab15c5e38715}{float32\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Coeffs}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{arm__math__types_8h_a4611b605e45ab401f02cab15c5e38715}{float32\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+State}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{block\+Size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialization function for the floating-\/point FIR interpolator. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em S} & points to an instance of the floating-\/point FIR interpolator structure. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em L} & upsample factor. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em num\+Taps} & number of filter coefficients in the filter. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em p\+Coeffs} & points to the filter coefficient buffer. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em p\+State} & points to the state buffer. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em block\+Size} & number of input samples to process per call. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The function returns ARM\+\_\+\+MATH\+\_\+\+SUCCESS if initialization is successful or ARM\+\_\+\+MATH\+\_\+\+LENGTH\+\_\+\+ERROR if the filter length {\ttfamily num\+Taps} is not a multiple of the interpolation factor {\ttfamily L}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
